# Thu May 19 23:27:03 AST 2005
#
# http://weather.noaa.gov/pub/data/products/dictionary.txt
#
###############################################################################
#
# GSC Product Directory
#
# Products, described by a combination of WMO heading and AWIPS identifier, are
# classified in terms of type and target directory.  This file defines the
# storage location of uniquely identified products.  A product received at
# the NWS Telecommunications Gateway Server Center is identified by its WMO
# heading and, if present, AWIPS identifier.  The products storage location
# is then determined by reading this file, matching the key (fields 1-4), and
# retrieving the type, target directory, and filename.
#
# Record Format - Colon (":") used to terminate each field within a record.
#                 '#' used to start a comment line.
#                 Blank lines are allowed.
#
# Fields and descriptions -
#
# Field 1 - TTAAii, taken from the WMO heading.
# Field 2 - CCCC, taken from the WMO heading.
# Field 3 - NNN, taken from the AWIPS identifier.
# Field 4 - XXX, taken from the AWIPS identifier.
# Field 5 - Type indicator
#
#	Type	Meaning
#
#	0	Product is to be ignored, target directory and filename
#               may be omitted.
#	1	Product contains UGC lines and $$ terminators and will be 
#               broken into zone or warning area files.  The product will be
#               stored in the supplied target directory (see field 6) with
#               the state or area two-character abbreviation appended as the
#               last directory level to the target directory.  The product
#               file name will be based on the UGC line(s) found in the
#               product.
#	2	Product does not contain UGC lines and should be stored as a
#		single file in the specified target directory with the
#               specified filename.
#
# Field 6 - Target directory, the directory (under pub) into which the product
#	    will be stored.
#
# Field 7 - File name used when storing product, used for Type 2 products
#	    only.  Type 1 products have a filename of the form xxtddd where
#           xx is the state/area abbreviation, t is either 'Z' to indicate
#           zone or 'C' to indicate county and ddd is the zone or county
#           number.
#
# Field 8 - Expiration time (in hours).  A value of * indicates no expiration.  
#	    Products with a non-zero expiration time will be removed from the
#           system that many hours after they expire (as indicated in the UGC)
#           or will be removed from the system that many hours after they are
#           received if they contain no UGC lines. Products with an expiration
#           time of 0 will be immediately removed when they expire.
#
###############################################################################
